		   NULL, " Perché mai dovrei... perdonarla?!", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



//　むしろ許してほしいのは俺の方だろ？＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　むしろ許してほしいのは俺の方だろ？！",
		   NULL, "Sono io che voglio essere perdonato!", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



//　俺の何が許されないんだよ！＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　俺の何が許されないんだよ！！",
		   NULL, "Quale parte di me non puoi perdonare?!", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }



//　俺は絶対に殺されないからな！＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　俺は絶対に殺されないからな！！",
		   NULL, "Non voglio essere ucciso!", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }


//　俺が許されないなら俺だって許さない￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　俺が許されないなら俺だって許さない。",
		   NULL, "Se tu non mi perdonerai, allora io non ti perdonerò.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//　...許さない＠許さない＠許さない＠許さない＠許さない＠許さない＠許さない＠許さない...！＠
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　…許さない、",
		   NULL, "... non ti perdonerò,", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "許さない、",
		   NULL, " non ti perdonerò,", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "許さない、",
		   NULL, " non ti perdonerò,", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "許さない、",
		   NULL, " non ti perdonerò,", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "許さない、",
		   NULL, " non ti perdonerò,", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "許さない、",
		   NULL, " non ti perdonerò,", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "許さない、",
		   NULL, " non ti perdonerò,", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "許さない…！！",
		   NULL, " non ti perdonerò...!!", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

//「前原さん＠　聞こえてるなら返事をして下さい＠...もしもーし！！￥
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#a59da9>大石</color>", NULL, "<color=#a59da9>Ooishi</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 11, "ps3/s01/11/120700426", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「前原さん？",
		   NULL, "\"Maebara-san?", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 11, "ps3/s01/11/120700427", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　聞こえてるなら返事をして下さい。",
		   NULL, " Se riesci a sentirmi, allora rispondi.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(3, 11, "ps3/s01/11/120700428", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…もしもーし！！」",
		   NULL, " ... pronto!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//☆幕間
